Everything was going smooth, but heck there was an inexperienced guy who was assigned to draw blood, he not only poked hard he wiggled and twisted the needle after the needle was in, he couldn't find the vein. He continues to look for the vein by tilting and moving the needle, I and to tell him to stop while my son began "ouch ouch". In the beginning, I had to tell him I can't do this alone, only then he called the cold face front office lady.

By then my 4YO was in great pain. And this front office  lady who was helping, what a robotic person, can't they talk to kids, don't they know what to say. Idiot's went for the left hand and my son began to resist, I had to hold him hard, and the lady too had to hold. What a waste of my insurance money, I just let my child be a Guinea pig.

Can't you talk to a child who you with your inexperience made him go through a traumatic experience.
Boo to labcorp attendants here.< /Text>

<text>A really amazing Texas style BBQ joint in East Los?! Oh yeah!

I'm a fan of delicious meats served up big. This family owned and ran business did not disappoint in portion or in how incredible everything was. I can tell there's a lot of love that they put into this place. From the food to the quite and laid back vibe, I enjoyed. Got the Pit Master Combo that's good enough to share or gorge on your own. It comes with a pork rib, chicken, Angus beef brisket, and a pull pork slider plus a choice of a side (went with the coleslaw).The brisket was nicely prepared, tender and juicy. It was my favorite on this huge plate. For the chicken they use leg and thigh. I could taste the smokiness from the skin on through to the meat. Pull pork is Texas size slider. They stuffed that bread with plenty of BBQ'd shredded meat. Just the sauces themselves shows that they are experts on how Texas BBQ (aside from their meat smoking skills) should taste. Excellent bold combinations of smoky, spicy and sweet. But not to overpower the amazing smoked flavors of the meats cause just a drizzle is all you're gonna really need.

A definite recommendation for anyone, from anywhere, wanting yummy Texas BBQ in SoCal.  One of the best I've had in this state. I say skip the corporate chain Lucille's and taste what truly is good ... in the hood ;) and support this wonderful, local, family owned gem. Double win.< /text>< userid>

< Review>
I been traveling miles and I mean miles for good Barbecue. I travel because East LA does not and has not had good BBQ. But I was wrong, for the last 6 years this small mom and pop joint has been making fantastic BBQ. I was skeptical when I walked in today, the owner gave ne a sample of the pulled pork with his slaw while I waited for our order. I fell in love with it from the first bite, it taste even better than it smells.
I can not praise the food enough, remember it is cash only and is cosy for a small group. Large groups best get it to go.
If ypu get pulled pork make sure you get the slaw, pairs perfect together. Sweet slaw balances the tangy bbq. Brisket is ridiculously delicious. And ribs are tender and perfectly done. I will let know about the chicken when I have room to try it.

I hope they blow up so they stay in business,  but hope not to big because I would hate to stand in line for an hour to get my food.</Review>

<Date>1520427041374<//Date>< resp>
None<//resp>
< Review>
Quite amazing BBQ in LA, my mom thinks it may be the best brisket we ever had.

It's a little place on Whittier and there is some free 1 hour parking on the street outside. The two owners are great to talk to and oh so friendly. We ordered 3 plates and 2 sodas and didn't reach $40.
The brisket was delicious (so much so that we ordered some more to go for later), not overly sauced, and the meat really shone through. Smoked chicken was juicy and flavourful, the ribs were meaty and the pulled pork (although listed as a slider, it's a sandwich in it's own right) was great - the meat was pulled but not stringy or too wet. Sides of macaroni salad and coleslaw were good, but the jalapeno corn bread was the item to go for (apparently not available on all days, so try your luck).
The man behind the counter was kind enough to make a hot green tea for my mum, not on the menu but from his private stash. Service like that, coupled with the food we got, makes this a place I wish I had heard about sooner. It's a 25 min drive from Los Feliz where we were staying but this was definitely worth it!< /Review>

< review>
Ok so I've been saying for years look out when East LA gets a good BBQ spot it's gonna blow up! Except this place however has yet to blow and for reasons I really can't explain. So here's my first experience the owner goes over the menu with me in detail simple, but he explains it to me with such passion. I get excited as he he sets the bar really high!

That said it takes allot for me to write a review just moments after I visit an establishment. In this case however it's a must. My order was to go the first thing I tried was the pulled pork sandwich which the owner recommended. Wow I gotta say not a pulled pork fan, but this guy got it right for some reason it's delicious! The potato wedges.... Well I'll pass in the future wasted real estate in my opinion. Other than that this place is a winner potato salad cooked to perfection Baked Beans ..... Decent!!

Now for all the money people lets talk about the ribs. I've tried many throughout my days and these are at least in my top five. Smokey, fall off the bone tender, with great sauce. So come out and support this little gem in East Los You'll be glad you did trust me 4 1/2 stars!!<//review>

<review>Clean and comfortable. Furniture seem like it was updated recently. Check in and out was quick and easy. Hand sanitizer is provided for each room.You should be warned that because of the way the building way laid out, it creates this wind cave with the parking lot. It can get quite loud in the morning with all the car traffic passing through Del Mar Ave. This could be an issue if you are a light sleeper and want to sleep in. This was not a problem at night since the traffic is way lighter.There's a mini side room attached to the main section of the room that has a sofa and nothing else. It would have been nice if there was a dinning table and 2 chairs in that room instead of a couch. Since the TV is in the main room in front of the bed, there's nothing to do in the side room. There is only 1 office chair for the desk, so if you want to get take out/eat in your hotel room and you are staying with more than one person, you will have to take turns sharing the chair to eat at the desk. The 2 things I mentioned above weren't that big of a deal to me. Overall Travelodge Rosemead location is a great place to stay on a budget< /review><response>None< /response><GmapID>0x80c2daa5f22552bb:0xd61103148c9e926f< /GmapID>< UserId.>

< date>
1573749915848<//date>
< Text>
So first I'd like to say if you are reading this review and expecting the Ritz or Hilton, please don't bother. This is a budget hotel option for travelers. Now if you have that in mind and are still looking at staying, than you'll see my review and rating makes sense!

To give you an idea, I am an outside sales rep whose territory is pretty much ALL of SoCal. I had an event last night in Carpenteria, and had to be in La Canada in the early AM. Rather than drive to my home in Orange County, I figured a local option may be best. Well...for those who have traveled in LA before...local options are not cheap at all. You pretty much need to plan to spend over $100 a night which for me, I just needed a bed, a shower, and maybe a quick snack in the AM. Lots of those options under $100 sadly were either too far away, or reviews were EXTREMELY poor. Then I find this gem! Not to say it doesn't have it's flaws even for a budget location, but here is the GOOD, the BAD, and the UGLY

Good
It's affordable! Hoteltonight had an even bigger discount for the last minute reservation. On top of that, free Wi-Fi and Free Parking! Free continental as well so I was happy, and it was in a nice area centrally located near my appointments so it was an easy transition. Plus, rooms were recently renovated and looked really nice! Don't let the outside shell fool you, and for those worried about the safety of parking you vehicle, well Rosemead is actually a pretty safe neighborhood in most places. Plus, they FLOOD LIGHT the parking lot! Thank god for black out blinds, but it made me feel safe at 1 AM.

Bad
My room was on the second floor and in the corner so I had a pretty big room with a little nook as well. The nook had no desk, but the entrance did. I'd probably move some stuff around to the nook as it seems odd to just have a couch only. The bed creaked and wasn't the best, but I was exhausted and slept fine as long as I didn't move too much. Came with essentials like soap and shampoo, and again for the price and the fact that I just needed a place for less than 10 hours, not bad. My only other complaint would be the towels. They didn't have full size towels, only hand towels and wash rags. I didn't call downstairs since again...1 AM, but maybe bring a towel just in case.

Ugly
My ONLY Ugly would be the toilet. It made noise ALL NIGHT and morning. Had to close the bathroom door which solved the problem. Literally, didn't really hear it at all until I opened the door again that morning. Not sure if this was just in my room (231) or all the others, but needless to say wasn't fun at first.

Overall a great experience! Again didn't bother management cause it was 1 AM and wasn't expecting the most amazing stay, but to my surprise for the type of establishment it was, and the price, I was very much impressed! This will be my go to should I have any appointments in LA and need a place to stay! Basic accommodations and amazing price!< /Text>

<Review>(Translated by Google) Well, it's ok. The school grade 3 describes it best.
It's a motel and it's cheap so don't come here with too high expectations. We stayed 2 nights and it was good for that ..
It's not super clean, but neither is it dirty (and I'm sensitive to that). Fridge and microwave are available and work. The kitchen is there as a separate room, but without dishes (I didn't ask about them either). The kitchen wasn't really clean, so I wouldn't have cooked anyway. Bed is comfortable, linen was clean. Bathroom was ok. There were no bugs or anything like that. We were up on the first floor.
The staff is very nice. In the morning there are a few packaged sweets and coffee from a rather calcified coffee pot downstairs in the narrow reception room, which tastes amazingly good.
During the day we were out anyway. It is also not a place where you spend the day and go on vacation. I wouldn't book here for that.

Parking lot is large and in the courtyard, so you can see the car from the room window.
Despite the glass at the reception, I felt safe as a woman here. It was seldom to see anyone either in the inner courtyard or outside on the street, actually never .. that is clearly a part of the city where you don't walk but drive everywhere by car.
There are many single-family houses with small gardens in the area. No ghetto or similar not even begin to .. the Walmart 6 min. from the hotel is super sorted.

The only really negative point because of which I subtract the 2nd star is WiFi. That didn't work at all and we were accommodated above the reception. Every 2 min. the connection broke off, you had to log in again, re-enter your password, etc. Really exhausting and annoying.

Otherwise ok for 1-3 nights!

< review>
Love this park! Hands down ome of my kids favorite parks. They love they play structure that resembles a rocket/space ship. They have swings for big kids and babies, they have a splash pad and an ample amount of running room. Tons of picnic areas, so a great place to have a party, they have the splash pad which is a huge plus especially in the summer. They also have a section for dogs, which is also fun for the kids.
